So, if you cannot get a phone signal, you can still read the data on the physical smartcard or access the basic details from the virtual smartcard’s QR Code that proves the smartcard is genuine. \r\n\r\n\r\nUsage details for the Windows Mobile version:\r\n\r\nPlease note that this app requires newer models of the Lumia range, which use the enhanced NFC chipset (PN547) e.g. Lumia 735 or 830. Older Lumia models, even with NFC, will not be able to read a card (unfortunately, the app is unable to detect this condition, and is therefore not able to warn the user that the card cannot be read).\r\n\r\nTo read a physical smartcard:\r\n\r\n1.\tMake sure that NFC is enabled on your device;\r\n2.\tOpen the app;\r\n3.\tHold a smartcard to the back, near the top, of your device;\r\n4.\tAn image of the card appears. (If the photo shown does not match the one shown on the front of the actual card, it has probably been tampered with and may be a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the Card Details tab to view the list of current qualifications.\r\n6.\tDo the same with more smartcards if you need to.\r\n\r\n\r\nTo read a virtual smartcard:\r\n\r\n1.\tOpen the app;\r\n2.\tTouch the 'SCAN A QR CODE' button;\r\n3.\tRead the QR code (from approx. 10cm away);\r\n4.\tAn image of the card appears. (If the photo shown does not match the one on the cardholder’s phone, it is a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the card image to view the back of the card;\r\n6.\tTouch the Core Data tab to view qualifications;\r\n7.\tTouch the SkillSight tab, if one is present, to view further qualifications for the cardholder;\r\n8.\tRepeat this process to read more virtual smartcards. \r\n\r\n\r\nAdditional functionality and settings accessed via the drop-down menu are:\r\n\r\n1.\tCard List - shows all the cards you have read;\r\na.\tSort – by date, name or expiry date;\r\nb.\tFilter – by today, last 3 days, last week, last month and all cards;\r\nc.\tDelete – remove entries;\r\ne.\tExport Swipes – select an export file format (XML or CSV);\r\nf.\tDashboard – takes you back to the main dashboard.\r\n2.\tOptions:\r\na.\tSave Images – save an image of the smartcard (front and back) into your pictures folder;\r\nb.\tExport Folder – specify where you want to save the exported files;\r\nc.\tDefault Export Email – add an email address to send your export files to;\r\nd.\tMy Device Name – add a friendly device name that will be used to identify this device
